###########################
# Annexation Events concerning Asia & Oceania
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file
###########################

# Table of Contents
#	This might sound arcane to you, but we are folliwng a center-west-north-east-south route. You'll get the hang of it
#
# Central Asia
#		Kazakhstan
#		Turkestan
#			Bukhara
#			Khiva
#	Afghanistan
#
# Northern Asia
#	Siberia
#	Far Eastern Russia
#
# Eastern Asia
#	China
#		Tibet
#		Xinjiang
#		Mongolia
#			Tuva
#		Manchuria
#		Legation Cities
#	Korea
#	Japan
#		Sakhalin
#	Taiwan
#
# South-East Asia
#	Siam
#	Indochina
#		Vietnam
#		Laos
#		Cambodia
#	Philippines
#	Indonesia
#	Papua New Guinea
#	Malaysia
#		Sarawak
#
# South Asia
#	Central India
#		Maharashtra
#		Gujarat
#		Rajputana
#		Khalistan
#		Kashmir
#		Sikkim
#		Assam
#		Bengal
#		Orissa
#		Chhatisgarh
#		Vizagapatnam
#		Hyderabad
#		Andhra
#		Madras
#		Mysore
#		Punjab
#		Baluchistan
#		Quetta
#		Sind
#	Nepal
#	Bhutan
#	Burma
#		Kachin
#		Shan
#	Ceylon
#
# Oceania
#	Australia
#	New Zealand
#	Hawaii

add_namespace = annex

#####################################
##     C E N T R A L   A S I A     ##
#####################################

country_event = { #Fate of Kazakhstan
	id = annex.3001
	title = annexation_810
	desc = annexation_810_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annexations_reset_central_asian_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						571 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Omsk
						407 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Tashkent
						861 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Khorezm
					}
					RUS_socialists_can_integrate = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					571 = { #Omsk
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:571.owner = { save_event_target_as = russia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					407 = { #Tashkent
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:russia }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:407.owner = { save_event_target_as = turkestan }
			}
			418 = { retain_state = yes } #Ashkhabad
			1042 = { retain_state = yes } #Badakhshan
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.3001.a"
		name = annex.3001.a
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = russia
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:russia = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
				OR = {
					is_major = no
					is_ally_with = event_target:russia
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = turkestan
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:turkestan = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
				OR = {
					is_major = no
					is_ally_with = event_target:turkestan
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KAZ }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate united Central Asia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.asia.release_united_central_asia"
		name = annex.asia.release_united_central_asia
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				407 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Tashkent
				861 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Khorezm
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = event_target:united_central_asia }
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = russia
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:russia = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
				OR = {
					is_major = no
					is_ally_with = event_target:russia
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = turkestan
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:turkestan = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
				OR = {
					is_major = no
					is_ally_with = event_target:turkestan
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KAZ }
		annexations_release_united_central_asia = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Russia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.give_to_russia"
		name = annex.give_to_russia
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = russia
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:russia = { is_russian_tag = yes }
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:russia }
				is_ally_with = event_target:turkestan
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:turkestan = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:russia = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:russia }
		KAZ = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Turkestan
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.asia.give_to_turkestan"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_turkestan
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = turkestan
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:turkestan = { is_russian_tag = yes }
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = russia
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:russia = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:turkestan }
				is_ally_with = event_target:russia
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:russia = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:turkestan = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:turkestan }
		KAZ = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_annex = yes
		}
		KAZ = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
							owner = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
						}
					}
				}
				add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to overlord
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.give_to_overlord"
		name = annex.give_to_overlord
		trigger = {
			annexations_should_give_lands_to_overlord = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = overlord }
		KAZ = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #Cancel
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.cancel"
		name = annex.cancel
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	after = {
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Turkestan
	id = annex.3002
	title = annexation_407
	desc = annexation_407_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annexations_reset_central_asian_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							583 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Petropavlovsk
							owns_any_state_of = {
								589 #Semireche
								861 #Khorezm
							}
						}
						589 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Semireche
						861 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Khorezm
						732 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Samarkand
					}
					RUS_socialists_can_integrate = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					589 = { #Semireche
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:589.owner = { save_event_target_as = alash }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					861 = { #Khorezm
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:alash }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:861.owner = { save_event_target_as = khiva }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					732 = { #Samarkand
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:alash }
							NOT = { tag = event_target:khiva }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:732.owner = { save_event_target_as = bukhara }
			}
			418 = { retain_state = yes } #Ashkhabad
			1042 = { retain_state = yes } #Badakhshan
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.3002.a"
		name = annex.3002.a
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ally_with = event_target:alash
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:alash = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ally_with = event_target:khiva
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:khiva = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ally_with = event_target:bukhara
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:bukhara = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate united Central Asia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.asia.release_united_central_asia"
		name = annex.asia.release_united_central_asia
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				405 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Bukhara
				810 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Semipalatinsk
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = event_target:united_central_asia }
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ally_with = event_target:alash
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:alash = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ally_with = event_target:khiva
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:khiva = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ally_with = event_target:bukhara
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:bukhara = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		annexations_release_united_central_asia = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Alash/Russia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.asia.give_to_alash"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_alash
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = alash
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:alash = { is_russian_tag = yes }
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:alash }
				is_ally_with = event_target:khiva
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:khiva = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:alash }
				is_ally_with = event_target:bukhara
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:bukhara = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:alash = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:alash }
		TRK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Khiva
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.asia.give_to_khiva"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_khiva
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = khiva
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:khiva = { is_russian_tag = yes }
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:khiva }
				is_ally_with = event_target:alash
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:alash = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:khiva }
				is_ally_with = event_target:bukhara
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:bukhara = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:khiva = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:khiva }
		TRK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Bukhara
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.asia.give_to_bukhara"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_bukhara
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = bukhara
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:bukhara = { is_russian_tag = yes }
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:bukhara }
				is_ally_with = event_target:alash
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:alash = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:bukhara }
				is_ally_with = event_target:khiva
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:khiva = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:bukhara = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:bukhara }
		TRK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_annex = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				583 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Petropavlovsk
				589 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no } #Semireche
			}
			KAZ = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
								owner = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
							}
						}
					}
					add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}
		TRK = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
							owner = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
						}
					}
				}
				add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to overlord
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.give_to_overlord"
		name = annex.give_to_overlord
		trigger = {
			annexations_should_give_lands_to_overlord = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = overlord }
		TRK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
	}

	option = { #Cancel
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3002 option annex.cancel"
		name = annex.cancel
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	after = {
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Bukhara
	id = annex.3003
	title = annexation_405
	desc = annexation_405_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annexations_reset_central_asian_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							583 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Petropavlovsk
							owns_any_state_of = {
								407 #Tashkent
								861 #Khorezm
							}
						}
						407 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Tashkent
						861 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Khorezm
					}
					RUS_socialists_can_integrate = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					407 = { #Tashkent
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:407.owner = { save_event_target_as = turkestan }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					861 = { #Khorezm
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:turkestan }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:861.owner = { save_event_target_as = khiva }
			}
			418 = { retain_state = yes } #Ashkhabad
			1042 = { retain_state = yes } #Badakhshan
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.3003.a"
		name = annex.3003.a
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = khiva
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
					event_target:khiva = { is_russian_tag = no }
				}
				OR = {
					is_major = no
					is_ally_with = event_target:khiva
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = turkestan
				OR = {
					is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no

country_event = { #Fate of Afghanistan
	id = annex.3007
	title = annexation_267
	desc = annexation_267_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			AFG = { AFG_remove_monarchy = yes }
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { state = 267 } #Kabul
						NOT = { state = 415 } #Herat
						NOT = { state = 442 } #Peshawar
					}
					remove_core_of = AFG
				}
				else = {
					add_core_of = AFG
				}
				remove_claim_by = AFG
			}
			442 = { retain_state = yes } #Peshawar
			if = {
				limit = { tag = PER }
				add_state_claim = 415 #Herat
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #republic
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3007 option annex.3007.a"
		name = annex.3007.a
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}

			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}

				factor = 0.5
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AFG }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #monarchy

		name = annex.3007.b
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

			}

		}
		else = {
			var:tag_to_release = { AFG_create_amanullah = yes }
		}
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3007 option annex.give_to_overlord"

		}

	id = annex.3010

	desc = annexation_613_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

			determine_chinese_ally = yes

						is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes

					}
					add_claim_by = LEC
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = no }

			has_event_target = china

		}

	id = annex.3016
	title = annexation_743
	desc = annexation_743_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			LEC = { clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = LEC
						AND = {
							original_tag = JAP
							is_subject = no
							NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china }
						}
						china_is_potential_government = yes
						596 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Qiantang
						613 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Jinling
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = no }
				annexations_create_legation_cities_event_target = yes
				determine_chinese_ally = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_event_target = china } }
					if = {
						limit = {
							596 = { #Qiantang
								annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
								owner = {
									NOT = { tag = event_target:legation_cities }
									ROOT_can_grant_land_ignore_ideology = yes
								}
							}
						}
						var:596.owner = { save_event_target_as = china_qiantang }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							613 = { #Jinling
								annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
								owner = {
									NOT = { tag = event_target:legation_cities }
									NOT = { tag = event_target:china_qiantang }
									ROOT_can_grant_land_ignore_ideology = yes
								}
							}
						}
						var:613.owner = { save_event_target_as = china_jinling }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Legation Cities
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3016 option annex.3016.a"
		name = annex.3016.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = LEC }
			has_socialist_government = no
			is_chinese_tag = no
			is_subject = no
			NOT = { has_event_target = japan_forced_return }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = no
				is_american_tag = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:legation_cities }
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = event_target:china_qiantang
					is_ally_with = event_target:china_jinling
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LEC }
		743 = { #Shanghai
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			transfer_state_without_overriding_occupation = yes
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		LEC_puppet_setup = yes
	}

	option = { #Release China
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3016 option annex.china.release_china"
		name = annex.china.release_china
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = china_release_target
			NOT = { has_event_target = japan_forced_return }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china_release_target }
		743 = { remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes } #Shanghai
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { var:tag_to_release = { original_tag = FNG } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = var:tag_to_release
				autonomy_state = special_autonomous_dependency
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = JAP }
			clr_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china
			var:tag_to_release = { add_ideas = unequal_treaties_japan }
		}
		var:tag_to_release = { china_puppet_setup = yes }
	}

	option = { #Give to LEC
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3016 option annex.china.give_to_lec"
		name = annex.china.give_to_lec
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = legation_cities
			is_chinese_tag = no
			NOT = { has_event_target = japan_forced_return }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = no
				is_american_tag = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:legation_cities }
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = event_target:china_qiantang
					is_ally_with = event_target:china_jinling
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:legation_cities }

	}

state_event = { #Fate of Sakhalin
	id = annex.3019
	title = annexation_537
	desc = annexation_537_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							536 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Hokkaido
							ROOT = { owns_state = 537 } #South Sakhalin
						}
						AND = {
							OR = {
								408 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Vladivostok
								560 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Nikolayevsk
							}
							ROOT = { owns_state = 577 } #North Sakhalin
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					536 = { #Hokkaido
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							537 = { annexations_required_state_is_owned_by_either_side = yes } #South Sakhalin
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:536.owner = { save_event_target_as = japan }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					408 = { #Vladivostok
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:japan }
							577 = { annexations_required_state_is_owned_by_either_side = yes } #North Sakhalin
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:408.owner = { save_event_target_as = russia_vladivostok }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					560 = { #Nikolayevsk
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:japan }
							NOT = { tag = event_target:russia_vladivostok }
							577 = { annexations_required_state_is_owned_by_either_side = yes } #North Sakhalin
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes

		}

				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:japan }
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = event_target:russia_vladivostok
						is_ally_with = event_target:russia_nikolayevsk
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:japan = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:japan }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #scoped for the tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { state = 577 } #North Sakhalin
			537 = { transfer_if_owned = yes } #South Sakhalin
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to Russian tag 1 (owner of Vladivostok)

country_event = { #Fate of Rajputana
	id = annex.3035
	title = annexation_433
	desc = annexation_433_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			RJS = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes
			}
			annexations_reset_indian_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_indian_unifier_tag = yes
						AND = {
							original_tag = PJB
							owns_state = 440 #East Punjab
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					936 = { #Gwalior
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_indian_unifier_tag = yes
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:936.owner = { save_event_target_as = india }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:891.owner = { #West Punjab
						NOT = { tag = event_target:india }
						original_tag = PJB
						owns_state = 440 #East Punjab
						ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
					}
				}
				var:891.owner = { save_event_target_as = punjab }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #release as HND
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.asia.release_republican_india"
		name = annex.asia.release_republican_india
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_republican_india = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = mtth:annexations_release_republican_india_AI_weight
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HND }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #release as PRF
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.asia.release_princely_india"
		name = annex.asia.release_princely_india
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_princely_india = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = mtth:annexations_release_princely_india_AI_weight
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PRF }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #release as RAJ
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.asia.release_british_india"
		name = annex.asia.release_british_india
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_british_india = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = mtth:annexations_release_british_india_AI_weight
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RAJ }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #puppet RJS
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.3035.a"
		name = annex.3035.a
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_indian_splinters = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RJS }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_rajasthan = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = var:tag_to_release }
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to India
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.asia.give_to_india"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_india
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = india
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_release_any_india = yes
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:india }
				is_ally_with = event_target:punjab
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_give_to_britain_instead = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:india = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:india }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_rajasthan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Punjab
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.asia.give_to_punjab"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_punjab
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = punjab
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_release_any_india = yes
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:punjab }
				is_ally_with = event_target:india
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_give_to_britain_instead = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:punjab = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:punjab }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_rajasthan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Split between India and Punjab
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.3035.b"
		name = annex.3035.b
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = punjab
			has_event_target = india
			433 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Rajputana
			839 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Aravali
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_release_any_india = yes
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_ally_with = event_target:punjab
						NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:india }
					}
					AND = {
						is_ally_with = event_target:india
						NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:punjab }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						event_target:punjab = { is_subject = no }
						event_target:india = { is_subject = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						event_target:punjab = { is_subject = yes }
						event_target:india = { is_subject = no }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_give_to_britain_instead = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:punjab }
		433 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Rajputana

		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:india }
		839 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Aravali
	}

	option = { #Give to Britain
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.give_to_britain"
		name = annex.give_to_britain
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = britain
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:britain = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:britain }
		annexations_give_india_to_target = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to overlord
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.give_to_overlord"
		name = annex.give_to_overlord
		trigger = {
			annexations_should_give_lands_to_overlord = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = overlord }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_rajasthan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Annex
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_annex = yes
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_rajasthan = yes }
			add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Cancel
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3035 option annex.cancel"
		name = annex.cancel
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	after = {
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of East Punjab
	id = annex.3036
	title = annexation_440
	desc = annexation_440_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			KHA = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes
			}
			annexations_reset_indian_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_indian_unifier_tag = yes
						original_tag = PJB
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			annexations_create_indian_event_targets = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:891.owner = { #West Punjab
						original_tag = PJB
						NOT = { tag = event_target:india }
						NOT = { tag = event_target:india_princely }
						NOT = { tag = event_target:india_british }
						ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
					}
				}
				var:891.owner = { save_event_target_as = punjab }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #release as HND
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3036 option annex.asia.release_republican_india"

		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RAJ }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #puppet KHA
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3036 option annex.3036.a"
		name = annex.3036.a
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_bengal_punjab = yes
			NOT = { country_exists = KHA }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KHA }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_khalistan = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = var:tag_to_release }
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to HND
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3036 option annex.asia.give_to_india"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_india
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = india
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_release_any_india = yes
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:india }
				is_ally_with = event_target:punjab
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_give_to_britain_instead = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1

	option = { #Annex
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3036 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_annex = yes
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_khalistan = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { original_tag = PJB }
				}
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Cancel
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3036 option annex.cancel"
		name = annex.cancel
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	after = {
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Kashmir
	id = annex.3037
	title = annexation_441
	desc = annexation_441_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			KAS = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes
			}
			annexations_reset_indian_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						890 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Simla
						891 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #West Punjab
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					890 = { #Simla
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:890.owner = { save_event_target_as = india }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:891.owner = { #West Punjab
						original_tag = PJB
						NOT = { tag = event_target:india }
						ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
					}
				}
				var:891.owner = { save_event_target_as = punjab }
			}
			897 = { retain_state = yes } #Aksai Chin
		}
	}

	option = { #release as HND
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3037 option annex.asia.release_republican_india"
		name = annex.asia.release_republican_india
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_republican_india = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = mtth:annexations_release_republican_india_AI_weight
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HND }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #release as PRF
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3037 option annex.asia.release_princely_india"
		name = annex.asia.release_princely_india
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_princely_india = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = mtth:annexations_release_princely_india_AI_weight
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PRF }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #release as RAJ
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3037 option annex.asia.release_british_india"
		name = annex.asia.release_british_india
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_british_india = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = mtth:annexations_release_british_india_AI_weight
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RAJ }
		annexations_release_india = yes
	}

	option = { #puppet KAS
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3037 option annex.3037.a"
		name = annex.3037.a
		trigger = {
			annexations_can_release_bengal_punjab = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KAS }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_kashmir = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = var:tag_to_release }
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to HND
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3037 option annex.asia.give_to_india"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_india
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = india
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_release_any_india = yes
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {

	desc = annexation_888_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						323 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Nepal
						324 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Bhutan
						887 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Darjeeling
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					323 = { #Nepal
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:323.owner = { save_event_target_as = nepal }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					324 = { #Bhutan
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:nepal }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:324.owner = { save_event_target_as = bhutan }

							NOT = { tag = event_target:bhutan }

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						424 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Andhra
						426 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Orissa
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					424 = { #Andhra
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:424.owner = { save_event_target_as = andhra }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					426 = { #Orissa
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:andhra }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:426.owner = { save_event_target_as = orissa }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to owner of Andhra
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3043 option annex.asia.give_to_owner_of_andhra"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_owner_of_andhra
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = andhra
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:andhra }
				is_ally_with = event_target:orissa
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:andhra = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:andhra }
		889 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Vizagapatnam
	}

	option = { #Give to owner of Orissa
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3043 option annex.asia.give_to_orissa"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_orissa
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = orissa
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:orissa }
				is_ally_with = event_target:andhra
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:orissa = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:orissa }
		889 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Vizagapatnam
	}

	option = { #Give to overlord

					}
				}

			if = {

					annexations_india_is_puppet_or_independent_ally_of_ROOT = no
					429 = { #Bombay
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:india }
							NOT = { tag = event_target:india_princely }
							NOT = { tag = event_target:india_british }
							NOT = { tag = event_target:punjab }

						is_indian_unifier_tag = yes
						425 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Mysore
					}

							NOT = { tag = event_target:india_british }

						}
					}
				}

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = no }
				818 = { retain_state = yes } #Pondicherry
			}
			281 = { retain_state = yes } #Maldives

					}

							NOT = { tag = event_target:persia }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes

					}

country_event = { #Fate of Ceylon
	id = annex.3057
	title = annexation_422
	desc = annexation_422_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ceylon = no
						NOT = { state = 707 } #Mauritius
						NOT = { state = 709 } #Seychelles
					}
					remove_core_of = CEY
				}
				else = {
					add_core_of = CEY
				}
				remove_claim_by = CEY
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {

							is_indian_unifier_tag = yes
							naval_base > 0

			annexations_create_non_puppet_britain_event_target = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_event_target = india }
					annexations_is_ally_of_entente_britain = no
				}

					limit = {
						HND = {
							naval_base > 0
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}

country_event = { #Fate of Australia
	id = annex.3058
	title = annexation_285
	desc = annexation_285_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = AST
				if = {
					limit = { is_australia = yes }
					add_core_of = AST
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = AST
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = NZL } }
				every_state = {
					remove_claim_by = NZL
					if = {
						limit = { is_new_zealand = yes }
						add_core_of = NZL
					}
					else = {
						remove_core_of = NZL
					}
				}
			}
			AST = {
				remove_ideas = {
					AST_british_advisors_idea
					AST_uob_advisors_idea
					AST_anderson_doctrine_idea
					AST_new_guard_military_1
					AST_new_guard_military_2
					AST_new_guard_economy_1
					AST_new_guard_economy_2
					AST_rising_power
					AST_totalist_economy_idea
					AST_AFM_economy_1
					AST_AFM_economy_2
				}
				AST_become_republic = yes
			}
			annexations_create_non_puppet_britain_event_target = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				GEA = { country_event = { id = austral.373 days = 20 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Australia or united Australasia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3058 option annex.3058.a"
		name = annex.3058.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:KR_king_base }
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_give_to_britain_instead = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		if = {
			limit = { 284 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } } #North Island
			NZL = { every_core_state = { remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes } }
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		AST_puppet_setup = yes
	}

	option = { #Release Australia and New Zealand
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3058 option annex.3058.b"
		name = annex.3058.b
		trigger = {
			284 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #North Island
			NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:KR_king_base }
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_give_to_britain_instead = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NZL }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		NZL_puppet_setup = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line

country_event = { #Fate of New Zealand
	id = annex.3060
	title = annexation_284
	desc = annexation_284_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = NZL
				if = {
					limit = { is_new_zealand = yes }
					add_core_of = NZL
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = NZL
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = AST }
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:KR_king_base = {
						is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
						is_subject = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { AST = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes } }
					AST = { save_event_target_as = britain }
				}
				else = {
					event_target:KR_king_base = { save_event_target_as = britain }
				}
			}
			else = {
				annexations_create_australia_event_target = yes
				annexations_create_non_puppet_britain_event_target = yes

				factor = 0
				has_event_target = australia

	id = annex.3061

	desc = annexation_629_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = HAW
				if = {
					limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
					add_core_of = HAW
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = HAW
				}
			}
			HAW = {
				clr_country_flag = HAW_can_join_factions
				HAW_remove_monarchy = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						385 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Oregon
						original_tag = JAP
						original_tag = GEA
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					385 = { #Oregon
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:385.owner = { save_event_target_as = united_states }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_american_tag = no
					is_ally_with = event_target:united_states
				}
				save_event_target_as = AI_dont_annex

			annexations_create_german_east_asia_event_target = yes
			annexations_create_japan_event_target = yes
			638 = { retain_state = yes } #Guam
			726 = { retain_state = yes } #Samoa

	}

			is_subject = no
			is_american_tag = no
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HAW }

			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = HAW_monarchy_restoration }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_monarchy_restoration
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_completed_focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
					has_completed_focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Hawaii as a monarchy

country_event = { #Fate of Tawang
	id = annex.3070
	title = annexation_858
	desc = annexation_858_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						432 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Assam
						693 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Chamdo
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					432 = { #Assam
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:432.owner = { save_event_target_as = india }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					693 = { #Chamdo
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:india }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:693.owner = { save_event_target_as = tibet }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to India

state_event = { #Fate of the Pacific Islands
	id = annex.3071
	title = annexation_633
	desc = annexation_633_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ROOT = { original_tag = AST }
						ROOT = { original_tag = NZL }
						ROOT = { original_tag = GEA }
						ROOT = { original_tag = JAP }
						ROOT = { is_american_tag = yes }
						if = {
							limit = { is_french_colonial_claim = yes }
							ROOT = { annexations_france_can_annex_overseas = yes }
						}
						else = {
							ROOT = { annexations_britain_can_annex_overseas = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							state = 647 #Palau
							627 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Mindanao
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_actual_major = yes }
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
				save_event_target_as = AI_dont_annex
			}
			annexations_create_australia_event_target = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NZL = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes } }
				NZL = { save_event_target_as = new_zealand }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					state = 647 #Palau
					627 = {
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				PHI = { save_event_target_as = philippines }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					385 = { #Oregon
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:385.owner = { save_event_target_as = united_states }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_french_colonial_claim = yes }
				annexations_create_non_socialist_france_event_target = yes
			}
			else = {
				annexations_create_non_socialist_britain_event_target = yes
			}
			annexations_create_japan_event_target = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					GEA = {
						is_subject = yes
						overlord = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:GEA.overlord = { save_event_target_as = germany }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { GEA = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes } }
				GEA = { save_event_target_as = germany }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Australia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3071 option annex.oceania.give_to_australia"
		name = annex.oceania.give_to_australia
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = australia
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_AI_wants_to_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:australia }
					OR = {
						has_event_target = new_zealand
						AND = {
							is_ally_with = event_target:philippines
							event_target:philippines = { is_in_asia = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:australia }
					annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_ally_with = event_target:philippines
							event_target:philippines = { is_in_asia = no }
						}
						is_ally_with = event_target:united_states
						is_ally_with = event_target:britain
						is_ally_with = event_target:france
						is_ally_with = event_target:germany
						is_ally_with = event_target:japan
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = france
				is_french_colonial_claim = yes
				ROOT = { annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = britain
				is_british_colonial_claim = yes
				ROOT = { annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:australia = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:australia }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #scoped for the tooltip

state_event = { #Fate of the Legation Ports
	id = annex.3074
	title = annexation_326
	desc = annexation_326_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ROOT = { original_tag = LEC }
						ROOT = { original_tag = GEA }
						ROOT = {
							original_tag = JAP
							is_subject = no
							NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china }
						}
						AND = {
							state = 326 #Hong Kong
							ROOT = { annexations_britain_can_annex_overseas = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							state = 728 #Guangzhouwan
							ROOT = { annexations_france_can_annex_overseas = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							state = 729 #Macau
							ROOT = { annexations_portugal_can_annex_overseas = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							state = 745 #Dalian
							ROOT = {
								OR = {
									is_russian_tag = yes
									original_tag = JAP
								}
								has_socialist_government = no
								is_subject = no
							}
						}
						any_neighbor_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						is_subject = no
						is_chinese_tag = no
					}
				}
				annexations_create_legation_cities_event_target = yes
				annexations_create_german_east_asia_event_target = yes
				if = {
					limit = { state = 326 } #Hong Kong
					annexations_create_non_socialist_britain_event_target = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state = 728 } #Guangzhouwan
					annexations_create_non_socialist_france_event_target = yes
				}

					limit = { state = 729 } #Macau
					annexations_create_non_socialist_portugal_event_target = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { is_subject = no } }
				determine_chinese_ally = yes
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						is_possible_legation_cities_state = no
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:legation_cities }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land_ignore_ideology = yes }
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_one }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						is_possible_legation_cities_state = no
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:legation_cities }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_one }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land_ignore_ideology = yes }
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_two }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = { #should never exist, but just in case
					limit = {
						is_possible_legation_cities_state = no
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:legation_cities }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_one }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_two }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land_ignore_ideology = yes }
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_three }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 85
			modifier = {

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = { has_subject = event_target:german_east_asia }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = { annexations_AI_will_consider_returning_colonies = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

state_event = { #Fate of Inner Mongolia
	id = annex.3075
	title = annexation_348
	desc = annexation_348_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						1114 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Gobi Desert
						ROOT = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							NOT = { original_tag = MAN }
						}
						ROOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = LEC_china }
					}
					any_neighbor_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { is_subject = no } }
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							1114 = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes } #Gobi Desert
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = mongolia }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:mongolia }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							NOT = { original_tag = MAN }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_one }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:mongolia }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_one }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							NOT = { original_tag = MAN }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_two }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:mongolia }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_one }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_two }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							NOT = { original_tag = MAN }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_three }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Mongolia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3075 option annex.china.give_to_mongolia"
		name = annex.china.give_to_mongolia
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = mongolia
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:mongolia }
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = event_target:china_one
						is_ally_with = event_target:china_two
						is_ally_with = event_target:china_three
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { 612 = { is_owned_by = event_target:mongolia } }
				NOT = { state = 612 } #Northern Chahar
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:mongolia = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:mongolia }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #scoped for the tooltip

state_event = { #Fate of the Tibetan Borderlands
	id = annex.3076
	title = annexation_353
	desc = annexation_353_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						748 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Tsonyi
						ROOT = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
						ROOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = LEC_china }
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							state = 604 #Xining
							ROOT = { owns_state = 353 } #Yushu
						}
						AND = {
							state = 353 #Yushu
							ROOT = { owns_state = 604 } #Xining
						}
						any_neighbor_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { is_subject = no } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						state = 604 #Xining
						748 = { #Tsonyi
							annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
							owner = {
								353 = { annexations_required_state_is_owned_by_either_side = yes } #Yushu
								ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
							}
						}
					}
					var:748.owner = { save_event_target_as = tibet }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { state = 604 } #Xining
						748 = { #Tsonyi
							annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
							owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
						}
					}
					var:748.owner = { save_event_target_as = tibet }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:tibet }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_one }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:tibet }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_one }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_two }
				}
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:tibet }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_one }
						NOT = { is_owned_by = event_target:china_two }
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							is_chinese_tag = yes
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
					owner = { save_event_target_as = china_three }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Tibet
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3076 option annex.china.give_to_tibet"
		name = annex.china.give_to_tibet
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = tibet
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:tibet }
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = event_target:china_one
						is_ally_with = event_target:china_two
						is_ally_with = event_target:china_three
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:tibet = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:tibet }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #scoped for the tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { state = 604 } #Xining
			353 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Yushu
		}
	}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:china }
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = event_target:turkestan
					is_ally_with = event_target:afghanistan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:china = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china }
		1042 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Badakhshan
	}

	option = { #Give to owner of Kabul
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3084 option annex.asia.give_to_afghanistan"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_afghanistan
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = afghanistan
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				annexations_can_annex = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_ally_with = event_target:afghanistan }
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = event_target:china
					is_ally_with = event_target:turkestan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:afghanistan = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:afghanistan }
		1042 = { transfer_state_and_notify = yes } #Badakhshan
	}

	option = { #Give to overlord

		name = annex.give_to_overlord
		trigger = {
			annexations_should_give_lands_to_overlord = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = overlord }

	option = { #Annex

		}

	}

	option = { #Cancel

		name = annex.cancel
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	after = {
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of the Malabar Coast
	id = annex.3085
	title = annexation_1034
	desc = annexation_1034_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						423 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Madura
						425 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Mysore
						867 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Travancore
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					423 = { #Madura
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
					}
				}
				var:423.owner = { save_event_target_as = madura }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					425 = { #Mysore
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:madura }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:425.owner = { save_event_target_as = mysore }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					867 = { #Travancore
						annexations_state_owner_is_valid_grant_target = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = event_target:madura }
							NOT = { tag = event_target:mysore }
							ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
						}
					}
				}
				var:867.owner = { save_event_target_as = travancore }
			}
		}
	}

					is_ally_with = event_target:mysore
					is_ally_with = event_target:travancore
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1

			}
		}
